% Ans        : MultiAns
% File       : 0003
% Sub        : Theorems-EVT
% Topic      : Derivative
% Type       : Concept

\ProblemFileHeader{500}
\ifquestionPull
\ifproblemToFind\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0003. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\lbrace\begin{array}{ll}
\log\left(-x\right)\; , & x<-1\\[3pt]
{\left(x + 2\right)}^{4}\; , & x\geq-1
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[-16,12]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%%

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0003. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\lbrace\begin{array}{ll}
\log\left(-x + 3\right)\; , & x<2\\[3pt]
{\left(x - 1\right)}^{5}\; , & x\geq2
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[1,18]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

\begin{problem}

\log\left(-x + 2\right)\; , & x<1\\[3pt]
x^{4}\; , & x\geq1
\end{array}\right.\]

 \choice{Yes}

 \end{multipleChoice}

\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

{\left(x + 8\right)}^{4}\; , & x\geq-7
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[-20,3]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\lbrace\begin{array}{ll}
\log\left(-x - 4\right)\; , & x<-5\\[3pt]
{\left(x + 6\right)}^{3}\; , & x\geq-5
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[-12,12]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[-14,-4]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

 over the interval $[-3,17]$?

 \begin{multipleChoice}

 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

\begin{multipleChoice}

\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}

\latexProblemContent{
\ifVerboseLocation This is Derivative Concept Question 0003. \\ \fi
\begin{problem}

Does the Extreme Value Theorem hold for the function \[f(x)=\left\lbrace\begin{array}{ll}
\log\left(-x + 2\right)\; , & x<1\\[3pt]
x^{8}\; , & x\geq1
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[-16,8]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}

{\left(x + 4\right)}^{10}\; , & x\geq-3
\end{array}\right.\]
 over the interval $[-4,2]$?

\input{Derivative-Concept-0003.HELP.tex}
 
 \begin{multipleChoice}
 \choice{Yes}
 \choice[correct]{No}
 \end{multipleChoice}

If not, which condition fails?

\begin{multipleChoice}
\choice[correct]{$f$ is not continuous on the interval}
\choice{The interval is not closed}
\choice{$f$ is not differentiable on the interval}
\choice{Nothing fails; the theorem holds}
\end{multipleChoice}
\end{problem}
}
